setup_op90 = {

	set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Inventory_Array_Initial_0 = 54 } # Days of Food Left
	set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Inventory_Array_Initial_1 = 54 } # Days of Fuel Left

	set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Inventory_Array_Initial_3 = 5 } # Survival Equipment

		array = global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Scope_Array
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { global.Antarctica_GUI_Tile_Scope_Array^i = AAA }

		}

setup_op90_playtest = {
	set_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Selected_Tucker
	clr_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Active_Incident_Complete
	set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Active_Incident = 19 }
	run_op90_incident_19_setup = yes
}

show_op90_temp = {
	set_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Active
}

hide_op90_temp = {
	clr_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Active
}

run_op90_backend = {
	# NOTE - Runs hourly
	
	# No game overs
	set_variable = { Antarctica_Militarization = 75 }
	set_variable = { Antarctica_Legitimacy = 75 }
	set_variable = { Antarctica_Equipment = 75 }
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Mechanic_Paused }
		}
		# Update hour of day
		add_to_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Hours = 1 }
		set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Hour_Of_Day = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Hours }
		modulo_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Hour_Of_Day = 24 }
		
		if = { # Stuff that happens only when traveling and time is passing
			limit = {
				check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Travel_Speed_KMH > 0 }
			}
			# Daily checks
			if = {
				limit = {
					set_temp_variable = { mod = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Hours }
					modulo_temp_variable = { mod = 24 }
					check_variable = { mod = 0 }
				}
				# None currently
			}
			
			# Move expedition forwards
			if = { # Stop for 0500 breakfast, 1200 lunch, 1800 dinner, 2300-0500 sleep
				limit = {
					OR = {
						check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Hour_Of_Day = 5 }
						check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Hour_Of_Day = 12 }
						check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Hour_Of_Day = 18 }
						
						check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Hour_Of_Day = 23 }
						check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Hour_Of_Day = 0 }
						check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Hour_Of_Day = 1 }
						check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Hour_Of_Day = 2 }
						check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Hour_Of_Day = 3 }
						check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Hour_Of_Day = 4 }
					}
				}
				#add_to_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Traveled_KM = 0 }
				set_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Travel_Resting
			}
			else = {
				clr_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Travel_Resting
				add_to_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Traveled_KM = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Travel_Speed_KMH }
			}
			
			# Check for base arrival
			if = { # Sobral 1
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Reached_Sobral_1 }
					check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Traveled_KM > 419 }
				}
				set_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Reached_Sobral_1
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Traveled_KM = 420 }
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Timer = 72 }
		
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Travel_Speed_KMH = 0 }
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Travel_Resume = 96 }
				
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_AAC_Intelligence
					}
					country_event = antarctica_aaa_op90.190
				}
				else = {
					country_event = antarctica_aaa_op90.140
				}
			}
			else_if = { # Pole
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Reached_Pole }
					check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Traveled_KM > 1489 }
				}
				set_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Reached_Pole
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Traveled_KM = 1490 }
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Timer = 72 }
		
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Travel_Speed_KMH = 0 }
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Travel_Resume = 24 }
				
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Crew_Dead = 0 }
				for_each_loop = {
					array = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Array
					value = v
					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^v = 16 }
						}
						add_to_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Crew_Dead = 1 }
					}
				}
				
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_AAC_Intelligence }
						check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Crew_Dead = 0 }
					}
					country_event = antarctica_aaa_op90.340
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_AAC_Intelligence
							check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Crew_Dead < 4 }
						}
					}
					country_event = antarctica_aaa_op90.350
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Crew_Dead < 8 }
					}
					country_event = antarctica_aaa_op90.360
				}
				else = {
					country_event = antarctica_aaa_op90.370
				}
			}
			else_if = { # Sobral 2
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Reached_Sobral_2 }
					check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Traveled_KM > 2559 }
				}
				set_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Reached_Sobral_2
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Traveled_KM = 2560 }
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Timer = 72 }
		
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Travel_Speed_KMH = 0 }
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Travel_Resume = 24 }
				
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_AAC_Intelligence
					}
					country_event = antarctica_aaa_op90.420
				}
				else = {
					country_event = antarctica_aaa_op90.410
				}
			}
			else_if = { # Belgrano End
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Reached_Belgrano_End }
					check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Traveled_KM > 2979 }
				}
				set_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Reached_Belgrano_End
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Traveled_KM = 2980 }
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Timer = 72 }
		
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Travel_Speed_KMH = 0 }
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Travel_Resume = 9999 }
				
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Crew_Dead = 0 }
				for_each_loop = {
					array = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Array
					value = v
					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^v = 16 }
						}
						add_to_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Crew_Dead = 1 }
					}
				}
				
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Crew_Dead > 4 } }
					country_event = antarctica_aaa_op90.440
				}
				else = {
					country_event = antarctica_aaa_op90.430
				}
			}
			
			# Check incidents
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Active }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Timer = 0 }
					}
					clr_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Active_Incident_Complete
					random_list = {
						100 = { # Lucky you, no incident
							modifier = {
								factor = 1
								always = yes
							}
							modifier = {
								add = 0
								always = yes
							}
							
							set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Timer = 24 }
						}
						100 = { # Incident 1 - Foreign Patrol
							modifier = {
								add = var:Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_Total_Inv
								check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_Total_Inv > 0 }
							}
							modifier = {
								factor = 2.5
								check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Traveled_KM > 420 }
								check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Traveled_KM < 1490 }
								has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Foreign_Mission_Active_At_Start
							}
							modifier = {
								factor = 5
								has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Spotted_Foreign_Plane
							}
							
							set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Active_Incident = 1 }
							run_op90_incident_1_setup = yes
						}
						100 = { # Incident 2 - Blizzard
							modifier = {
								add = var:Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Days_Since_Last_Blizzard
								check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Days_Since_Last_Blizzard > 0 }
							}
							
							modifier = { # balance
								factor = 1.4
								always = yes
							}
							
							set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Active_Incident = 2 }
							run_op90_incident_2_setup = yes
						}
						100 = { # Incident 3 - Penguins
							modifier = {
								factor = 0
								AND = {
									check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Traveled_KM > 420 }
									check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Traveled_KM < 2560 }
								}
							}
							
							set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Active_Incident = 3 }
							run_op90_incident_3_setup = yes
						}
						100 = { # Incident 4 - Vehicle in Crevasse

							}

						}
						100 = { # Incident 9 - Snowcat Breaks Down
							modifier = {
								factor = 0
								check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Inventory_Array^6 = 0 }
							}
							modifier = {
								factor = 2
								has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Vehicle_Breakdown_Light
							}
							modifier = {
								factor = 5
								has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Vehicle_Breakdown_Heavy
							}
							modifier = {
								factor = 0.9

							modifier = {

						100 = { # Incident 10 - Impassable Terrain Encountered
							modifier = {

							modifier = {

							}

						100 = { # Incident 12 - Foreign Plane
							modifier = {
								add = var:Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_Total_Inv
								check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_Total_Inv > 0 }
							}
							modifier = {
								factor = 2.5
								AND = {
									check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Traveled_KM > 420 }
									check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Traveled_KM < 1490 }
									has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Foreign_Mission_Active_At_Start
								}
							}
							modifier = {
								factor = 0

							set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Active_Incident = 12 }

						100 = { # Incident 13 - Clear Weather
							modifier = {

							}

							run_op90_incident_13_setup = yes
						}
						100 = { # Incident 14 - Sled Breaks Down
							modifier = {
								factor = 0
								check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Inventory_Array^7 = 0 }

							modifier = {

							modifier = {

							}
							modifier = {
								add = 25
								AND = {
									check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Traveled_KM > 420 }
									check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Traveled_KM < 2560 }
								}
							}
							modifier = {
								add = 25
								AND = {
									check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Traveled_KM > 1290 }
									check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Traveled_KM < 1690 }
								}
							}
							
							set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Active_Incident = 15 }
							run_op90_incident_15_setup = yes

						100 = { # Incident 16 - Crew Member Snaps
							modifier = {
								factor = 0
								NOT = { is_in_array = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array = 10 } }
							}
							
							set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Active_Incident = 16 }
							run_op90_incident_16_setup = yes

						100 = { # Incident 17 - Dog Team Finds Good Route
							modifier = {

							modifier = {

								check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status^19 = 3 }
							}
							modifier = {

								check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Inventory_Array^8 = 0 }

						100 = { # Incident 18 - Crew Member Falls Into Crevasse
							modifier = {

							}
							
							set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Active_Incident = 18 }
							run_op90_incident_18_setup = yes
						}
						100 = { # Incident 19 - Crossing the Great Rift
							modifier = {
								factor = 0
								has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Crossed_Rift
							}
							modifier = {
								factor = 999999999
								NOT = { has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Crossed_Rift }

							run_op90_incident_19_setup = yes

							modifier = {
								factor = 10
								has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Desperate_Measures
							}
							
							set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Active_Incident = 20 }
							run_op90_incident_20_setup = yes
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					add_to_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Timer = -1 }
					clamp_variable = { var = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Timer min = 0 }
				}
			}
		}
		
		# Stuff that always happens when time is passing
		# Daily checks
		if = {
			limit = {
				set_temp_variable = { mod = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Hours }
				modulo_temp_variable = { mod = 24 }
				check_variable = { mod = 0 }
			}
			add_to_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Days = 1 }
			
			# Add to days since blizzard
			add_to_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Days_Since_Last_Blizzard = 1 }
			
			# Decrease food
			add_to_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Inventory_Array^0 = -1 }
			clamp_variable = { var = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Inventory_Array^0 min = 0 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Inventory_Array^0 > 0 }
				}
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Days_Without_Food = 0 }
			}
			else = {
				add_to_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Days_Without_Food = 1 }
			}
			# Decrease fuel
			add_to_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Inventory_Array^1 = -1 }
			clamp_variable = { var = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Inventory_Array^1 min = 0 }
	
			# Check for sickness
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Sickness_Counter > 0 }
				}
				add_to_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Sickness_Counter = -1 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Sickness_Counter = 0 }
				}
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Crew_Target = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Sickness_Member }
				randomize_variable = { var = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Crew_Hurt distribution = uniform min = 1 max = 60 }
				round_variable = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Crew_Hurt
				subtract_from_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Health_Array^Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Crew_Target = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Crew_Hurt }
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Injury_Array^Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Crew_Target = -1 }
				
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Sickness_Counter = -1 }
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Sickness_Member = -1 }
			}
			
			# Update statuses
			update_op90_statuses = yes
		}
		
		# Hourly checks
		# Animations
		update_op90_animations = yes
		
		# Events
		check_fire_op90_events = yes
		
		# Check to reset travel speed to default
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Travel_Resume = 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Travel_Speed_KMH = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Max_Travel_Speed_KMH }
			multiply_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Travel_Speed_KMH = 0.1 }
			round_variable = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Travel_Speed_KMH
			clamp_variable = { var = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Travel_Speed_KMH min = 1 }
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Travel_Resume = -1 }
			clr_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Travel_Stopped
		}
		else = {
			add_to_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Travel_Resume = -1 }
			clamp_variable = { var = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Travel_Resume min = -1 }

			if = { # Not moving
				limit = {
					check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Travel_Speed_KMH = 0 }
				}
				set_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Travel_Stopped
			}
		}
	}
}

run_op90_incident_1_setup = {
	# Probably always want to set speed to 0
	set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Travel_Speed_KMH = 0 }
	
	# Start anim
	set_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Snow_Wipe
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Foreign_Mission_Active_At_Start
		}
		clr_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Foreign_Mission_Active_At_Start
	}
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAO < Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAG }
			check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAO < Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAJ }
			check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAO < Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAC }
		}
		set_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Foreign_Patrol_AAO
		set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAO = 25 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAG < Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAO }
			check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAG < Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAJ }
			check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAG < Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAC }
		}
		set_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Foreign_Patrol_AAG
		set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAG = 25 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAJ < Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAG }
			check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAJ < Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAO }
			check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAJ < Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAC }
		}
		set_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Foreign_Patrol_AAJ
		set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAJ = 25 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAC < Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAG }
			check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAC < Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAJ }
			check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAC < Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAO }
		}
		set_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Foreign_Patrol_AAC
		set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAC = 25 }
	}
	else = {
		random_list = {
			1 = { set_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Foreign_Patrol_AAO }
			1 = { set_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Foreign_Patrol_AAG }
			1 = { set_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Foreign_Patrol_AAJ }
			1 = { set_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Foreign_Patrol_AAC }
		}
	}

	set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_Total = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAC }
	add_to_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_Total = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAJ }
	add_to_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_Total = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAG }
	add_to_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_Total = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAO }
	set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_Total_Inv = 100 }
	subtract_from_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_Total_Inv = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_Total }
	
	# Option 1 - Requirements - 1 Leadership, Modifiers - None, Effects - 2 Injured 3 Fuel 1 Dog if Fail, Modifiers - 2 Leadership (Works on the Germans and OAA always, Japanese with leadership skill)
	#set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Option_1_Skill_0 = 0 }
	set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Option_1_Effect_Crew = 2 }
	set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Option_1_Effect_1 = 5 }
	set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Option_1_Effect_9 = 1 }
	#for_each_loop = {
	#	array = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Array
	#	index = i

	# Option 2 - Requirements - 4 Driving, Modifiers - 4 Navigation, Effects - 1 Injured 2 Fuel if Fail, Modifiers - Improved Speed III (Works on all if tech is high enough)
	set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Option_2_Skill_7 = 0 }
	set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Option_2_Skill_5 = 0 }
	set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Option_2_Effect_Crew = 1 }
	set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Option_2_Effect_1 = 3 }

		array = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Array
		index = i
		value = v
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				meta_trigger = {
					text = {
						check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Skill_Array_[SKILL_ARRAY]^7 = 1 }
						OR = {

	set_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Snow_Wipe
	
	# Option 1
	set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Option_1_Skill_6 = 0 }
	set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Option_1_Effect_Crew = 3 }
	for_each_loop = {
		array = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Array
		index = i
		value = v
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				meta_trigger = {
					text = {
						check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Skill_Array_[SKILL_ARRAY]^6 = 1 }

run_op90_incident_1_outcome = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Selected_Option = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Foreign_Patrol_AAO
					has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Foreign_Patrol_AAG
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Foreign_Patrol_AAJ
						has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Option_1_Skill_0_Pass
					}
				}
			}
			# Nothing, all good
			for_each_loop = {
				array = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Array
				
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^v < 5 }
					}
				}
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^v = 17 }
			}
		}
		else = {
			subtract_from_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Inventory_Array^1 = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Option_1_Effect_1 }
			clamp_variable = { var = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Inventory_Array^1 min = 0 }

run_op90_incident_5_outcome = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Selected_Option = 1 }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Inventory_Array^3 = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Option_1_Cost_3 }
		clamp_variable = { var = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Inventory_Array^3 min = 0 }
		# Get amounts of supplies on one sled
		set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Option_1_Effect_0 = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Inventory_Array^0 }
		divide_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Option_1_Effect_0 = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Inventory_Array^7 }
		set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Option_1_Effect_1 = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Inventory_Array^1 }
		divide_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Option_1_Effect_1 = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Inventory_Array^7 }
		set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Option_1_Effect_2 = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Inventory_Array^2 }
		divide_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Option_1_Effect_2 = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Inventory_Array^7 }
		set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Option_1_Effect_3 = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Inventory_Array^3 }
		divide_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Option_1_Effect_3 = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Inventory_Array^7 }
		set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Option_1_Effect_4 = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Inventory_Array^4 }
		divide_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Option_1_Effect_4 = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Inventory_Array^7 }
		set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Option_1_Effect_5 = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Inventory_Array^5 }
		divide_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Option_1_Effect_5 = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Inventory_Array^7 }
		# Subtract lost fraction of supplies
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Option_1_Effect_Crew = 1 } }
			set_temp_variable = { loss_factor = 0.833 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Option_1_Effect_Crew = 2 } }
			set_temp_variable = { loss_factor = 0.666 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Option_1_Effect_Crew = 3 } }
			set_temp_variable = { loss_factor = 0.5 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Option_1_Effect_Crew = 4 } }
			set_temp_variable = { loss_factor = 0.333 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Option_1_Effect_Crew = 5 } }
			set_temp_variable = { loss_factor = 0.166 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Option_1_Effect_Crew = 6 } }
			set_temp_variable = { loss_factor = 0 }
		}
		multiply_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Option_1_Effect_0 = loss_factor }
		multiply_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Option_1_Effect_1 = loss_factor }
		multiply_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Option_1_Effect_2 = loss_factor }

		limit = {
			check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Selected_Option = 1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Foreign_Patrol_AAO
					has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Foreign_Patrol_AAG
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Foreign_Patrol_AAJ
						has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Option_1_Skill_0_Pass
					}
				}
			}

run_op90_incident_20_outcome = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Selected_Option = 1 }
		}
		
		set_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Gain_Food_On_Death
		
		set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Travel_Speed_KMH = 0 }
		set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Travel_Resume = 1 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Selected_Option = 2 }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Inventory_Array^5 = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Option_2_Cost_5 }
		clamp_variable = { var = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Inventory_Array^5 min = 0 }
		add_to_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Inventory_Array^0 = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Option_2_Effect_0 }
		clamp_variable = { var = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Inventory_Array^0 min = 0 }
		
		clr_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Gain_Food_On_Death
		
		set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Weakest_Member_ID = -1 }
		set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Weakest_Member_HP = 100 }
		for_each_loop = {
			array = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Array
			value = v
			index = i
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Health_Array^v < Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Weakest_Member_HP }
						check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Health_Array^v = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Weakest_Member_HP }
					}
				}
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Weakest_Member_ID = v }
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Weakest_Member_HP = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Health_Array^v }
			}
		}
		
		set_temp_variable = { status = 16 }
		set_temp_variable = { amount = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { target = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Weakest_Member_ID }
		apply_op90_status_effects = yes
		
		set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Travel_Speed_KMH = 0 }
		set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Travel_Resume = 1 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Selected_Option = 3 }
		}
		
		set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Travel_Speed_KMH = 0 }
		set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Travel_Resume = 1 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Selected_Option = 4 }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Inventory_Array^5 = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Option_4_Cost_5 }
		clamp_variable = { var = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Inventory_Array^5 min = 0 }
		add_to_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Inventory_Array^0 = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Option_4_Effect_0 }
		clamp_variable = { var = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Inventory_Array^0 min = 0 }
		
		clr_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Gain_Food_On_Death
		
		set_temp_variable = { status = 16 }
		set_temp_variable = { amount = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { target = -1 }
		apply_op90_status_effects = yes
		
		set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Travel_Speed_KMH = 0 }

	set_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Active_Incident_Complete
	clear_op90_incident_variables = yes

apply_op90_status_effects = {
	# parameters
	# status - which status to apply
	# amount - number of crew to apply the status to
	# target - optional, apply status to target crew member, -1 by default
	
	# Get number of crew members, start at -1 because index
	# Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Incident_Crew_Target
	set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Array_Size = -1 }
	for_each_loop = {
		array = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Array
		add_to_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Array_Size = 1 }
	}
	
	# In case no crew members can get a status, exit after 100 checks
	set_temp_variable = { exit = 0 }
	# Array for tracking already affected crew
	clear_array = already_chosen
	
	# Apply effect for each amount
	while_loop_effect = {
		limit = {
			AND = {
				check_variable = { amount > 0 }
				check_variable = { exit < 100 }
			}
		}
		
		# If target isn't set
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { target = -1 }
			}
			randomize_temp_variable = { var = target distribution = uniform min = 0 max = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Array_Size }
			round_temp_variable = target
			set_temp_variable = { target = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Array^target }
		}
		
		# Check to ensure new target
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { is_in_array = { already_chosen = target } }
			}
			# Apply status to target if target is applicable
			if = { # Dead
				limit = {
					check_variable = { status = 16 }
					# Not dead, not vital
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 16 } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { target = 0 } } # Leal
					NOT = { check_variable = { target = 1 } } # Giro
					NOT = { check_variable = { target = 17 } } # Pujato
					
					NOT = {
						AND = {
							NOT = { has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Reached_Sobral_1 }
							check_variable = { target = 4 } # Bulacio
						}
					}
				}
				
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 16 }
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Health_Array^target = 0 }
				
				add_to_temp_variable = { amount = -1 }
				add_to_array = { already_chosen = target }
			}
			else_if = { # Missing
				limit = {
					check_variable = { status = 15 }
					# Not missing, not dead, not vital
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 15 } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 16 } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { target = 0 } } # Leal
					NOT = { check_variable = { target = 1 } } # Giro
					NOT = { check_variable = { target = 17 } } # Pujato
					
					NOT = {
						AND = {
							NOT = { has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Reached_Sobral_1 }
							check_variable = { target = 4 } # Bulacio
						}
					}
				}
				
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 15 }
				
				add_to_temp_variable = { amount = -1 }
				add_to_array = { already_chosen = target }
				
				log = "[?target] marked missing, [?amount] left"
			}
			else_if = { # Unconscious
				limit = {
					check_variable = { status = 14 }
					# Not unconscious, not dead, not vital
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 14 } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 15 } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 16 } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { target = 0 } } # Leal
					NOT = { check_variable = { target = 1 } } # Giro
					NOT = { check_variable = { target = 17 } } # Pujato
					
					NOT = {
						AND = {
							NOT = { has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Reached_Sobral_1 }
							check_variable = { target = 4 } # Bulacio
						}
					}
				}
				
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 14 }
				
				add_to_temp_variable = { amount = -1 }
				add_to_array = { already_chosen = target }
			}
			else_if = { # Recovering
				limit = {
					check_variable = { status = 18 }
					# Not recovering, not missing, not dead
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 18 } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 15 } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 16 } }
				}
				
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 18 }
				
				add_to_temp_variable = { amount = -1 }
				add_to_array = { already_chosen = target }
			}
			else_if = { # Severely Frostbitten
				limit = {
					check_variable = { status = 13 }
					# Not severely frostbitten, not missing, not dead
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 13 } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 15 } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 16 } }
				}
				
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 13 }
				
				add_to_temp_variable = { amount = -1 }
				add_to_array = { already_chosen = target }
			}
			else_if = { # Frostbitten
				limit = {
					check_variable = { status = 12 }
					# Not frostbitten, not missing, not dead, not severely frostbitten
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 12 } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 15 } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 16 } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 13 } }
				}
				
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 12 }
				
				add_to_temp_variable = { amount = -1 }
				add_to_array = { already_chosen = target }
			}
			else_if = { # Starving
				limit = {
					check_variable = { status = 11 }
					# Not starving, not missing, not dead
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 11 } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 15 } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 16 } }
				}
				
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 11 }
				
				add_to_temp_variable = { amount = -1 }
				add_to_array = { already_chosen = target }
			}
			else_if = { # Mortally Wounded - Damages HP, status applied on update
				limit = {
					check_variable = { status = 9 }
				}
				
				randomize_temp_variable = { var = damage distribution = uniform min = 81 max = 99 }
				round_temp_variable = damage
				subtract_from_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Health_Array^target = damage }
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Injury_Array^target = -1 }
				
				add_to_temp_variable = { amount = -1 }
				add_to_array = { already_chosen = target }
			}
			else_if = { # Grievously Injured - Damages HP, status applied on update
				limit = {
					check_variable = { status = 8 }
				}
				
				randomize_temp_variable = { var = damage distribution = uniform min = 61 max = 80 }
				round_temp_variable = damage
				subtract_from_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Health_Array^target = damage }
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Injury_Array^target = -1 }
				
				add_to_temp_variable = { amount = -1 }
				add_to_array = { already_chosen = target }
			}
			else_if = { # Seriously Injured - Damages HP, status applied on update
				limit = {
					check_variable = { status = 7 }
				}
				
				randomize_temp_variable = { var = damage distribution = uniform min = 41 max = 60 }
				round_temp_variable = damage
				subtract_from_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Health_Array^target = damage }
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Injury_Array^target = -1 }
				
				add_to_temp_variable = { amount = -1 }
				add_to_array = { already_chosen = target }
			}
			else_if = { # Injured - Damages HP, status applied on update
				limit = {
					check_variable = { status = 6 }
				}
				
				randomize_temp_variable = { var = damage distribution = uniform min = 21 max = 40 }
				round_temp_variable = damage
				subtract_from_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Health_Array^target = damage }
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Injury_Array^target = -1 }
				
				add_to_temp_variable = { amount = -1 }
				add_to_array = { already_chosen = target }
			}
			else_if = { # Slightly Injured - Damages HP, status applied on update
				limit = {
					check_variable = { status = 5 }
				}
				
				randomize_temp_variable = { var = damage distribution = uniform min = 1 max = 20 }
				round_temp_variable = damage
				subtract_from_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Health_Array^target = damage }
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Injury_Array^target = -1 }
				
				add_to_temp_variable = { amount = -1 }
				add_to_array = { already_chosen = target }
			}
			else_if = { # Depressed
				limit = {
					check_variable = { status = 10 }
					# Not depressed, not missing, not dead, not unconscious, not frostbitten, not severely frostbitten
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 10 } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 15 } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 16 } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 14 } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 13 } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 12 } }
				}
				
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 10 }
				
				add_to_temp_variable = { amount = -1 }
				add_to_array = { already_chosen = target }
			}
			else_if = { # Invigorated
				limit = {
					check_variable = { status = 17 }
					# Not invigorated, not missing, not dead, not frostbitten, not severely frostbitten, in good health
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 17 } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 15 } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 16 } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 13 } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 12 } }
					OR = {
						check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 0 }
						check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 1 }
						check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 2 }
						check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 3 }
						check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 4 }
					}
				}
				
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 17 }
				
				add_to_temp_variable = { amount = -1 }
				add_to_array = { already_chosen = target }
			}
			else_if = { # Dismal
				limit = {
					check_variable = { status = 4 }
					# Not dismal, not missing, not dead, not frostbitten, not severely frostbitten, not depressed
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 4 } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 15 } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 16 } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 13 } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 12 } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 10 } }
				}
				
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 4 }
				
				add_to_temp_variable = { amount = -1 }
				add_to_array = { already_chosen = target }
			}
			else_if = { # Poor
				limit = {
					check_variable = { status = 3 }
					# Not poor, not missing, not dead, not frostbitten, not severely frostbitten, not depressed
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 3 } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 15 } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 16 } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 13 } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 12 } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 10 } }
				}
				
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 3 }
				
				add_to_temp_variable = { amount = -1 }
				add_to_array = { already_chosen = target }
			}
			else_if = { # Nominal
				limit = {
					check_variable = { status = 2 }
					# Not nominal, not missing, not dead, not frostbitten, not severely frostbitten, not depressed
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 2 } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 15 } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 16 } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 13 } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 12 } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 10 } }
				}
				
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 2 }
				
				add_to_temp_variable = { amount = -1 }
				add_to_array = { already_chosen = target }
			}
			else_if = { # Well
				limit = {
					check_variable = { status = 1 }
					# Not well, not missing, not dead, not frostbitten, not severely frostbitten, not depressed
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 1 } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 15 } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 16 } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 13 } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 12 } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 10 } }
				}
				
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 1 }
				
				add_to_temp_variable = { amount = -1 }
				add_to_array = { already_chosen = target }
			}
			else_if = { # Excellent
				limit = {
					check_variable = { status = 0 }
					# Not excellent, not missing, not dead, not frostbitten, not severely frostbitten, not depressed
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 0 } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 15 } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 16 } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 13 } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 12 } }
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 10 } }
				}
				
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^target = 0 }
				
				add_to_temp_variable = { amount = -1 }
				add_to_array = { already_chosen = target }
			}
		}
		
		add_to_temp_variable = { exit = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { target = -1 }
	}
	
	clear_array = already_chosen
	
	# Prevent Leal, Giro, Pujato from dying
	clamp_variable = {
		var = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Health_Array^0
		min = 10
	}
	clamp_variable = {
		var = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Health_Array^1
		min = 10
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Pujato_Dead }
		}
		clamp_variable = {
			var = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Health_Array^17
			min = 10
		}
	}
}

update_op90_statuses = {
	# Prevent Leal, Giro, Pujato from dying
	clamp_variable = {
		var = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Health_Array^0
		min = 10
	}
	clamp_variable = {
		var = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Health_Array^1
		min = 10
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Pujato_Dead }
		}
		clamp_variable = {
			var = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Health_Array^17
			min = 10
		}
	}
	
	# Update all members
	for_each_loop = {
		array = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Array
		index = i
		value = v # This is the index to check in the other arrays
		
		if = { # Dead - HP = 0 - Dead, Event effects
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Health_Array^v = 0 }
					check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Health_Array^v < 0 }
				}
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Gain_Food_On_Death
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^v = 16 } }
				}
				clr_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Gain_Food_On_Death
				add_to_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Inventory_Array^0 = 2 }
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Desperate_Measures }
					has_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_At_Desperate_Measures
				}
				country_event = antarctica_aaa_op90.550
			}
			
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^v = 16 }
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Health_Array^v = 0 }
		}
		else_if = { # Missing - Set by event - Event effects
			limit = {
				check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^v = 15 }
			}
			add_to_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_MIA_Counter = 1 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_MIA_Counter = 7 }
				}
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_MIA_Counter = 0 }
				for_each_loop = {
					array = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Array
					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^v = 15 }
						}
						set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^v = 16 }
						set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Health_Array^v = 0 }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = { # Unconscious - Set by event - Event effects
			limit = {
				check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^v = 14 }
			}
		}
		else_if = { # Recovering - Set by button in GUI - Gain HP
			limit = {
				check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Injury_Array^v > 0 }
			}
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^v = 18 }
			
			add_to_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Health_Array^v = 5 }
			clamp_variable = { var = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Health_Array^v max = 100 min = 0 }
			
			add_to_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Injury_Array^v = -1 }
		}
		else_if = { # Severely Frostbitten - Set by event - Lose HP
			limit = {
				check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^v = 13 }
				check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Injury_Array^v = -1 }
			}
			add_to_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Health_Array^v = -10 }
			clamp_variable = { var = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Health_Array^v max = 100 min = 0 }
		}
		else_if = { # Frostbitten - Set by event - Lose HP
			limit = {
				check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^v = 12 }
				check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Injury_Array^v = -1 }
			}
			add_to_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Health_Array^v = -5 }
			clamp_variable = { var = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Health_Array^v max = 100 min = 0 }
		}
		else_if = { # Starving - Set by no food - Lose HP
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^v = 11 }
					AND = {
						check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Inventory_Array^0 = 0 }
						check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Health_Array^v < 20 }
						check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Days_Without_Food = 1 }
					}
					AND = {
						check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Inventory_Array^0 = 0 }
						check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Health_Array^v < 40 }
						check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Days_Without_Food = 5 }
					}
					AND = {
						check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Inventory_Array^0 = 0 }
						check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Health_Array^v < 60 }
						check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Days_Without_Food = 10 }
					}
					AND = {
						check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Inventory_Array^0 = 0 }
						check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Health_Array^v < 80 }
						check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Days_Without_Food = 15 }
					}
					AND = {
						check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Inventory_Array^0 = 0 }
						check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Days_Without_Food = 20 }
					}
				}
			}
			if = { # If you get more food, just make depressed
				limit = {
					NOT = { check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Inventory_Array^0 = 0 } }
				}
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^v = 10 }
			}
			else = {
				add_to_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Health_Array^v = -4 }
				clamp_variable = { var = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Health_Array^v max = 100 min = 0 }
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^v = 11 }
			}
		}
		else_if = { # Mortally Wounded - 0 to 19 HP and Injured - Event effects
			limit = {
				check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Health_Array^v < 20 }
				check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Injury_Array^v = -1 }
			}
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^v = 9 }
		}
		else_if = { # Grievously Injured - 20 to 39 HP and Injured - Event effects
			limit = {
				check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Health_Array^v < 40 }
				check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Injury_Array^v = -1 }
			}
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^v = 8 }
		}
		else_if = { # Seriously Injured - 40 to 59 HP and Injured - Event effects
			limit = {
				check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Health_Array^v < 60 }
				check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Injury_Array^v = -1 }
			}
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^v = 7 }
		}
		else_if = { # Injured - 60 to 79 HP and Injured - Event effects
			limit = {
				check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Health_Array^v < 80 }
				check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Injury_Array^v = -1 }
			}
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^v = 6 }
		}
		else_if = { # Slightly Injured - 80 to 100 HP and Injured - Event effects
			limit = {
				check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Health_Array^v < 101 }
				check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Injury_Array^v = -1 }
			}
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^v = 5 }
		}
		else_if = { # Depressed - Set by event - Event effects
			limit = {
				check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^v = 10 }
			}
		}
		else_if = { # Invigorated - Set by event - Event effects
			limit = {
				check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^v = 17 }
			}
		}
		else_if = { # Dismal - 0 to 19 HP - Event effects
			limit = {
				check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Health_Array^v < 20 }
			}
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^v = 4 }
		}
		else_if = { # Poor - 20 to 39 HP - Event effects
			limit = {
				check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Health_Array^v < 40 }
			}
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^v = 3 }
		}
		else_if = { # Nominal - 40 to 59 HP - Event effects
			limit = {
				check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Health_Array^v < 60 }
			}
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^v = 2 }
		}
		else_if = { # Well - 60 to 79 HP - Event effects
			limit = {
				check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Health_Array^v < 80 }
			}
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^v = 1 }
		}
		else_if = { # Excellent - 80 to 100 HP - Event effects
			limit = {
				check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Health_Array^v < 101 }
			}
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Members_Status_Array^v = 0 }
		}
	}
}

		multiply_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Travel_Offset_y = -80 }
		round_variable = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Travel_Offset_y
		
		set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Map_Expedition_Dot_x = 407 }
		add_to_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Map_Expedition_Dot_x = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Travel_Offset_x }
		set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Map_Expedition_Dot_y = 760 }
		add_to_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Map_Expedition_Dot_y = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Travel_Offset_y }
	}
	else_if = { # Belgrano
		limit = {
			check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Traveled_KM > 2980 }
		}
		add_to_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Map_Expedition_Dot_x = 449 }
		add_to_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Op90_Map_Expedition_Dot_y = 680 }
	}
}

calculate_AAA_Progressbar_Display = {
	clamp_variable = {
		var = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAO
		max = 25
		min = 0
	}
	clamp_variable = {
		var = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAG
		max = 25
		min = 0
	}
	clamp_variable = {
		var = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAJ
		max = 25
		min = 0
	}
	clamp_variable = {
		var = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAC
		max = 25
		min = 0
	}
	clamp_variable = {
		var = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_Total
		max = 100
		min = 0
	}
	
	set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAC_Display = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAC }
	set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAJ_Display = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAC }
	add_to_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAJ_Display = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAJ }
	set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAG_Display = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAC }
	add_to_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAG_Display = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAJ }
	add_to_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAG_Display = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAG }
	set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAO_Display = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAC }
	add_to_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAO_Display = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAJ }
	add_to_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAO_Display = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAG }
	add_to_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAO_Display = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAO }

	set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_Total = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAC }
	add_to_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_Total = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAJ }
	add_to_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_Total = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Mission_Secrecy_AAG }

}

calculate_AAA_research_decrease_timers = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Researching > -1 }
		}
		add_to_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status_Timer^Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Researching = -1 }
	}
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status_Timer^Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Researching = 0 }
			check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Researching > -1 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Researching = 0 }
				}
			}
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status^15 = 1 }
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status_Arrow^19 = 1 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Researching = 1 }
				}
			}
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status^2 = 1 }
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status^3 = 1 }
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status_Arrow^0 = 2 }
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status_Arrow^1 = 2 }
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status_Arrow^2 = 2 }
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status_Arrow^3 = 1 }
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status_Arrow^4 = 1 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Researching = 2 }
				}
			}
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status^4 = 1 }
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status_Arrow^3 = 2 }
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status_Arrow^5 = 1 }
			
			# XOR Stuff
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status^3 = 0 }
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status_Arrow^4 = 0 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Researching = 3 }
				}
			}
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status^5 = 1 }
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status_Arrow^4 = 2 }
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status_Arrow^6 = 1 }
			
			# XOR Stuff
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status^2 = 0 }
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status_Arrow^3 = 0 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Researching = 4 }
				}
			}
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status^6 = 1 }
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status_Arrow^5 = 2 }
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status_Arrow^8 = 1 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Researching = 5 }
				}
			}
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status^6 = 1 }
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status_Arrow^6 = 2 }
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status_Arrow^7 = 1 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Researching = 6 }
				}
			}
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status^7 = 1 }
			if = { # Fine Tune Engine for Fuel Use
				limit = {
					check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status^4 = 3 }
				}
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status_Arrow^8 = 2 }
			}
			else = { # Fine Tune Engine for Reliability
				set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status_Arrow^7 = 2 }
			}
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status_Arrow^9 = 1 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Researching = 7 }
				}
			}
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status_Arrow^9 = 2 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Researching = 8 }
				}
			}
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status^9 = 1 }
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status^10 = 1 }
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status_Arrow^10 = 2 }
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status_Arrow^11 = 2 }
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status_Arrow^12 = 2 }
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status_Arrow^13 = 1 }
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status_Arrow^14 = 1 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Researching = 9 }
				}
			}
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status^11 = 1 }
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status_Arrow^13 = 2 }
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status_Arrow^15 = 1 }
			
			# XOR Stuff
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status^10 = 0 }
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status_Arrow^14 = 0 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Researching = 10 }
				}
			}
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status^12 = 1 }
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status_Arrow^14 = 2 }
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status_Arrow^16 = 1 }
			
			# XOR Stuff
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status^9 = 0 }
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status_Arrow^13 = 0 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Researching = 11 }
				}
			}
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status^13 = 1 }
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status_Arrow^15 = 2 }
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status_Arrow^17 = 1 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Researching = 12 }
				}
			}
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status^14 = 1 }
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status_Arrow^16 = 2 }
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status_Arrow^18 = 1 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Researching = 13 }
				}
			}
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status_Arrow^17 = 2 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Researching = 14 }
				}
			}
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status_Arrow^18 = 2 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Researching = 15 }
				}
			}
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status^16 = 1 }
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status_Arrow^19 = 2 }
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status_Arrow^20 = 1 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Researching = 16 }
				}
			}
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status^17 = 1 }
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status_Arrow^20 = 2 }
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status_Arrow^21 = 1 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Researching = 17 }
				}
			}
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status^18 = 1 }
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status_Arrow^21 = 2 }
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status_Arrow^22 = 1 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Researching = 18 }
				}
			}
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status^19 = 1 }
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status_Arrow^22 = 2 }
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status_Arrow^23 = 1 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Researching = 19 }
				}
			}
			set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status_Arrow^23 = 2 }
		}
		
		set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Status^Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Researching = 3 }
		set_variable = { Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Tech_Researching = -1 }
		set_country_flag = Antarctica_GUI_AAA_Research_Window_Finished_Popup_Visible
	}
}
